I was surprised that the breakfast here at the hotel is delivered to the room, so there is no need to get up early and go to the restaurant. The breakfast delivery service is also very considerate. In general, the experience of staying in this time is very good, next time If you have a plan to come to Chengdu, this shop is the first choice!
